\doxysubsection{详细描述}
\subsubsection*{template$<$class RCU, typename Key, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$\newline
class cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}
\doxylink{struct_hash}{Hash} map based on multi-\/level array 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_container_FeldmanHashMap_rcu}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_container_FeldmanHashMap_rcu}%
 Source\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}2013\mbox{]} Steven Feldman, Pierre La\+Borde, Damian Dechev "{}\+Concurrent Multi-\/level Arrays\+:          Wait-\/free Extensible Hash Maps"{}
\end{DoxyItemize}

See algorithm short description \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_cds_container_FeldmanHashMap_hp}{here}

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Two important things you should keep in mind when you\textquotesingle{}re using {\ttfamily Feldman\+Hash\+Map}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item all keys is converted to fixed-\/size bit-\/string by hash functor provided. You can use variable-\/length keys, for example, {\ttfamily std\+::string} as a key for {\ttfamily Feldman\+Hash\+Map}, but real key in the map will be fixed-\/size hash values of your keys. For the strings you may use well-\/known hashing algorithms like \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Secure_Hash_Algorithm}{\texttt{ SHA1, SHA2}}, \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MurmurHash}{\texttt{ Murmur\+Hash}}, \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CityHash}{\texttt{ City\+Hash}} or its successor \href{https://code.google.com/p/farmhash/}{\texttt{ Farm\+Hash}} and so on, which converts variable-\/length strings to fixed-\/length bit-\/strings, and such hash values will be the keys in {\ttfamily Feldman\+Hash\+Map}. If your key is fixed-\/sized the hash functor is optional, see {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1feldman__hashmap_1_1traits_a6fd68f42f98b81c6b74bf2e86462f0a2}{feldman\+\_\+hashmap\+::traits\+::hash}} for explanation and examples.
\item {\ttfamily Feldman\+Hash\+Map} uses a perfect hashing. It means that if two different keys, for example, of type {\ttfamily std\+::string}, have identical hash then you cannot insert both that keys in the map. {\ttfamily Feldman\+Hash\+Map} does not maintain the key, it maintains its fixed-\/size hash value.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
The map supports \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_container_FeldmanHashMap_rcu_iterators}{bidirectional thread-\/safe iterators}.

Template parameters\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily RCU} -\/ one of \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type}
\item {\ttfamily Key} -\/ a key type to be stored in the map
\item {\ttfamily T} -\/ a value type to be stored in the map
\item {\ttfamily Traits} -\/ type traits, the structure based on {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1feldman__hashmap_1_1traits}{feldman\+\_\+hashmap\+::traits}} or result of {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1feldman__hashmap_1_1make__traits}{feldman\+\_\+hashmap\+::make\+\_\+traits}} metafunction.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Before including {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\doxylink{intrusive_2feldman__hashset__rcu_8h}{cds/intrusive/feldman\+\_\+hashset\+\_\+rcu.\+h}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} you should include appropriate RCU header file, see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type} for list of existing RCU class and corresponding header files. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{head\+\_\+bits}{ = {\ttfamily 8}, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{array\+\_\+bits}{ = {\ttfamily 4}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Creates empty map 


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em head\+\_\+bits} & -\/ 2\textsuperscript{head\+\_\+bits} specifies the size of head array, minimum is 4. \\
\hline
{\em array\+\_\+bits} & -\/ 2\textsuperscript{array\+\_\+bits} specifies the size of array node, minimum is 2.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Equation for {\ttfamily head\+\_\+bits} and {\ttfamily array\+\_\+bits\+:} 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aec8eb035c4982677b0bac7198b1baa2d}{hash\_type}})\ *\ 8\ ==\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{head\_bits}}\ +\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{N}}\ *\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{array\_bits}}}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily N} is multi-\/level array depth. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a1022c506b70f02ba3a4981891071d5d4}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!````~FeldmanHashMap@{\texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~}FeldmanHashMap}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{begin()}{begin()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a1103280fe1358c0eaa4366bee5da7445} 
template$<$class RCU, typename Key, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae150eafa433112f4a575e33163f3bee1}{iterator}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::begin (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Returns an iterator to the beginning of the map 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_container_FeldmanHashMap_rcu_iterators}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_container_FeldmanHashMap_rcu_iterators}%
The map supports thread-\/safe iterators\+: you may iterate over the map in multi-\/threaded environment under explicit RCU lock. RCU lock requirement means that inserting or searching is allowed but you must not erase the items from the map since erasing under RCU lock can lead to a deadlock. However, another thread can call {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aa3ee7899e06db81229c214c794e5aa7e}{erase()}} safely while your thread is iterating.

\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} typical example is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{foo}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ...\ other\ fields}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds::urcu::gc<\ cds::urcu::general\_buffered<>}}>\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{rcu}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap<\ rcu,\ std::string,\ foo>}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{map\_type}};}

\end{DoxyCode}


Each iterator object supports the common interface\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item dereference operators\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3ce0a9b563219da994c9172fcd5e40ce}{value\_type}}\ [\textcolor{keyword}{const}]\ *\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{operator\ -\/>}}()\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{noexcept}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3ce0a9b563219da994c9172fcd5e40ce}{value\_type}}\ [\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{const}}]\ \&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{operator}}\ *()\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{noexcept}}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item pre-\/increment and pre-\/decrement. Post-\/operators is not supported
\item equality operators {\ttfamily ==} and {\ttfamily !=}. Iterators are equal iff they point to the same cell of the same array node. Note that for two iterators {\ttfamily it1} and {\ttfamily it2} the condition {\ttfamily  it1 == it2 } does not entail {\ttfamily  \&(\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}it1) == \&(\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}it2) }\+: welcome to concurrent containers
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
It is possible the item can be iterated more that once, for example, if an iterator points to the item in an array node that is being splitted. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_a3d5d4314119d7b5a7d3b01cd743ef3b4}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!begin@{begin}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{begin()}{begin()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_a3d5d4314119d7b5a7d3b01cd743ef3b4} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae150eafa433112f4a575e33163f3bee1}{iterator}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::begin (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Returns an iterator to the beginning of the map 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_cds_container_FeldmanHashMap_iterators}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_cds_container_FeldmanHashMap_iterators}%
The map supports thread-\/safe iterators\+: you may iterate over the map in multi-\/threaded environment. It is guaranteed that the iterators will remain valid even if another thread deletes the node the iterator points to\+: Hazard Pointer embedded into the iterator object protects the node from physical reclamation.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Since the iterator object contains hazard pointer that is a thread-\/local resource, the iterator should not be passed to another thread.
\end{DoxyNote}
Each iterator object supports the common interface\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item dereference operators\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3ce0a9b563219da994c9172fcd5e40ce}{value\_type}}\ [\textcolor{keyword}{const}]\ *\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{operator\ -\/>}}()\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{noexcept}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3ce0a9b563219da994c9172fcd5e40ce}{value\_type}}\ [\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{const}}]\ \&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{operator}}\ *()\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{noexcept}}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item pre-\/increment and pre-\/decrement. Post-\/operators is not supported
\item equality operators {\ttfamily ==} and {\ttfamily !=}. Iterators are equal iff they point to the same cell of the same array node. Note that for two iterators {\ttfamily it1} and {\ttfamily it2}, the conditon {\ttfamily  it1 == it2 } does not entail {\ttfamily  \&(\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}it1) == \&(\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}it2) }
\item helper member function {\ttfamily release()} that clears internal hazard pointer. After {\ttfamily release()} the iterator points to {\ttfamily nullptr} but it still remain valid\+: further iterating is possible.
\end{DoxyItemize}

During iteration you may safely erase any item from the set; \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_a414c6d3ba2b5b5ce60fe13058da9bdc0}{erase\+\_\+at()} function call doesn\textquotesingle{}t invalidate any iterator. If some iterator points to the item to be erased, that item is not deleted immediately but only after that iterator will be advanced forward or backward.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
It is possible the item can be iterated more that once, for example, if an iterator points to the item in array node that is being splitted. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{begin()}{begin()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/4]}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::clear (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Clears the map (non-\/atomic) 

The function unlink all data node from the map. The function is not atomic but is thread-\/safe. After {\ttfamily clear}() the map may not be empty because another threads may insert items. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_aba4f48c5bfed54132474917f5fced739}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!clear@{clear}}

Checks if the map is empty 

Emptiness is checked by item counting\+: if item count is zero then the map is empty. Thus, the correct item counting feature is an important part of the map implementation. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_a7bc82ed46098ff6974eb3f8f9f227912}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!empty@{empty}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Delete {\ttfamily key} from the map 

{\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0d481be32ef50ad00b5120585038b569}{key\+\_\+type}} must be constructible from value of type {\ttfamily K}. The function deletes the element with hash value equal to {\ttfamily \doxylink{structhash}{hash( key\+\_\+type( key ))}}

Return {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily key} is found and deleted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

RCU should not be locked. The function locks RCU internally. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_a76ef7bd414aa27c46db85d76b4c17f12}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!erase@{erase}}

Delete {\ttfamily key} from the map 

{\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0d481be32ef50ad00b5120585038b569}{key\+\_\+type}} must be constructible from value of type {\ttfamily K}. The function deletes the element with hash value equal to {\ttfamily \doxylink{structhash}{hash( key\+\_\+type( key ))}}

Delete {\ttfamily key} from the map 

The function searches an item with hash value equal to {\ttfamily \doxylink{structhash}{hash( key\+\_\+type( key ))}}, calls {\ttfamily f} functor and deletes the item. If {\ttfamily key} is not found, the functor is not called.

The functor {\ttfamily Func} interface\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{extractor}}\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the element found.

{\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0d481be32ef50ad00b5120585038b569}{key\+\_\+type}} must be constructible from value of type {\ttfamily K}.

Return {\ttfamily true} if key is found and deleted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise

RCU should not be locked. The function locks RCU internally. 函数调用图\+:

Deletes the element pointed by iterator {\ttfamily iter} 

Returns {\ttfamily true} if the operation is successful, {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

The function does not invalidate the iterator, it remains valid and can be used for further traversing. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a57703d1af2bf39815a17baf6e2183bff}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!extract@{extract}}

exempt\+\_\+ptr \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item from the map with specified {\ttfamily key} 

The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily \doxylink{structhash}{hash( key\+\_\+type( key ))}} in the map, unlinks it from the map, and returns a guarded pointer to the item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should NOT be locked. The function does not call the disposer for the item found. The disposer will be implicitly invoked when the returned object is destroyed or when its {\ttfamily release()} member function is called. Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_aca805315e36258395882da0312c415be} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_a6c2e89e628cc3bc0675a1db960e6dac6}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item from the map with specified {\ttfamily key} 

The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily \doxylink{structhash}{hash( key\+\_\+type( key ))}} in the map, unlinks it from the map, and returns a guarded pointer to the item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

The item extracted is freed automatically by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} when returned {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_a6c2e89e628cc3bc0675a1db960e6dac6}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_a6c2e89e628cc3bc0675a1db960e6dac6}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxylink{struct_find}{Find} the key {\ttfamily key} 

The function searches the item by its hash that is equal to {\ttfamily \doxylink{structhash}{hash( key\+\_\+type( key ))}} and calls the functor {\ttfamily f} for item found. The interface of {\ttfamily Func} functor is\+:

\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found.

The functor may change {\ttfamily item.\+second}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3ce0a9b563219da994c9172fcd5e40ce}{value\+\_\+type}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{structget}{\+::get}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the key {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

The function searches the item by its {\ttfamily hash} and returns the pointer to the item found. If {\ttfamily hash} is not found the function returns {\ttfamily nullptr}.

RCU should be locked before the function invocation. Returned pointer is valid only while RCU is locked.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_a6c2e89e628cc3bc0675a1db960e6dac6}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{structget}{\+::get}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the key {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

The function searches the item with a hash equal to {\ttfamily \doxylink{structhash}{hash( key\+\_\+type( key ))}} and returns a guarded pointer to the item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

It is safe when a concurrent thread erases the item returned as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_a6c2e89e628cc3bc0675a1db960e6dac6}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}. In this case the item will be freed later by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} automatically when {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_a6c2e89e628cc3bc0675a1db960e6dac6}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_a6c2e89e628cc3bc0675a1db960e6dac6}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses one GC\textquotesingle{}s guard which can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::get\+\_\+level\+\_\+statistics (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecds_1_1container_1_1feldman__hashmap_a509d59df6bd6c5b50ba683d921dc77ab}{feldman\+\_\+hashmap\+::level\+\_\+statistics}} $>$ \&}]{stat}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Collects tree level statistics into {\ttfamily stat} 

The function traverses the set and collects statistics for each level of the tree into {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1container_1_1feldman__hashset_a53ccc7bd7719d07a866a4cbcc78e9f1e}{feldman\+\_\+hashset\+::level\+\_\+statistics}} struct. The element of {\ttfamily stat}\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} represents statistics for level {\ttfamily i}, level 0 is head array. The function is thread-\/safe and may be called in multi-\/threaded environment.

Result can be useful for estimating efficiency of hash functor you use. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_a2dc49be3ca35379d1a5270776b77b0fc}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!get\_level\_statistics@{get\_level\_statistics}}

The function creates an element with {\ttfamily key} and default value, and then inserts the node created into the map.

Preconditions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0d481be32ef50ad00b5120585038b569}{key\+\_\+type}} should be constructible from a value of type {\ttfamily K}. In trivial case, {\ttfamily K} is equal to {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0d481be32ef50ad00b5120585038b569}{key\+\_\+type}}.

\end{DoxyItemize}

Returns {\ttfamily true} if inserting successful, {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

Inserts new element 

The function creates a node with copy of {\ttfamily val} value and then inserts the node created into the map.

Preconditions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0d481be32ef50ad00b5120585038b569}{key\+\_\+type}} should be constructible from {\ttfamily key} of type {\ttfamily K}.
\item The {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3ce0a9b563219da994c9172fcd5e40ce}{value\+\_\+type}} should be constructible from {\ttfamily val} of type {\ttfamily V}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the map, {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

The function locks RCU internally. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_a3d3be2f71347255615c70ff38f67332f}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K \&\&}]{key}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_eigen_solver___eigen_solver___matrix_type_8cpp_a77c224aa52b434918ce65c33175aa8ad}{V}} \&\&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new element 

The function creates a node with copy of {\ttfamily val} value and then inserts the node created into the map.

Preconditions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0d481be32ef50ad00b5120585038b569}{key\+\_\+type}} should be constructible from {\ttfamily key} of type {\ttfamily K}.
\item The {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3ce0a9b563219da994c9172fcd5e40ce}{value\+\_\+type}} should be constructible from {\ttfamily val} of type {\ttfamily V}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the map, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_affc91ce8b541746ed9d776308d1c629b}\index{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::FeldmanHashMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!insert\_with@{insert\_with}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{insert\_with()}{insert\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_affc91ce8b541746ed9d776308d1c629b}

template$<$typename K, typename Func$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K \&\&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new element and initialize it by a functor 

This function inserts new element with key {\ttfamily key} and if inserting is successful then it calls {\ttfamily func} functor with signature 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{item}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


The argument {\ttfamily item} of user-\/defined functor {\ttfamily func} is the reference to the map\textquotesingle{}s item inserted\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily item.\+first} is a const reference to item\textquotesingle{}s key that cannot be changed.
\item {\ttfamily item.\+second} is a reference to item\textquotesingle{}s value that may be changed.
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0d481be32ef50ad00b5120585038b569}{key\+\_\+type}} should be constructible from value of type {\ttfamily K}.

The function allows to split creating of new item into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item from {\ttfamily key};
\item insert new item into the map;
\item if inserting is successful, initialize the value of item by calling {\ttfamily func} functor
\end{DoxyItemize}

This can be useful if complete initialization of object of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a3ce0a9b563219da994c9172fcd5e40ce}{value\+\_\+type}} is heavyweight and it is preferable that the initialization should be completed only if inserting is successful.

The function locks RCU internally. 函数调用图\+:

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ac02caa60ba1f4dade643d9ff47b18d83} 
template$<$class RCU, typename Key, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename K, typename Func$>$ \\
std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Feldman\+Hash\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K \&\&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates data by {\ttfamily key} 

The operation performs inserting or replacing the element with lock-\/free manner.

If the {\ttfamily key} not found in the map, then the new item created from {\ttfamily key} will be inserted into the map iff {\ttfamily b\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true} (note that in this case the \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0d481be32ef50ad00b5120585038b569}{key\+\_\+type} should be constructible from type {\ttfamily K}). Otherwise, if {\ttfamily key} is found, it is replaced with a new item created from {\ttfamily key}. The functor {\ttfamily Func} signature\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{my\_functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{value\_type}}\ *\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_feldman_hash_map}{old}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the map
\item {\ttfamily old} -\/ old item of the map, if {\ttfamily nullptr} -\/ the new item was inserted
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change any fields of the {\ttfamily item.\+second}.

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if {\ttfamily key} already exists.

The function locks RCU internally.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
See \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting} 
\end{DoxyWarning}
